Please use our 7 day trial period to make sure the software meets your requirements before purchasing.\n\nAs three new Excel workbooks are generated by the comparison process, it is a good idea to close all open Excel workbooks before using DiffEngineX. Otherwise multiple open Excel documents may cause confusion.\n\nBy default, most options are turned off. One option you should turn on right away is \"Add Hyperlinks to aid navigation\" found on the Options dialog. This links the difference report to the two color highlighted workbook copies.\n\nTo compare two Excel spreadsheets, first open them using the two browse buttons on DiffEngineX's user interface. Clicking the links in the difference report will automatically bring to the front the relevant Excel cell found to differ.\n\nThis has taken a bit of work, but now you have a good view of all the differences.\n\nFunctionality under the Tools menu will allow you to compare two folders of Excel spreadsheets against each other.
